1a1(1): sgra thams cad kyi snang ba ston pa/ dbang rdzogs pa rang byung chen po'i rgyud bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgya gar skad du/ kA yA lo kod+deSh+Ta b+hi Shiny+tsA ma hA swa yaM b+hA tan+t+ra nA ma/ bod skad du/ sku thams cad kyi snang ba ston pa/ dbang rdzogs pa rang byung chen po'i rgyud ces bya ba/ bcom
1b2(1): ldan 'das dbang thams cad kyi bdag nyid pad+ma he ru ka la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis bstan pa'i dus gcig na/ rig pa'i snang ba yongs su gsal ba'i gzhal yas na/
1b3(1): rig pa'i rtsal gyi dbang gi mnga' bdag des/ 'di skad ces bstan to// snang ba'i rig pa khyad par can// kun tu snang ba rnams nyon cig/ rig pa'i gnas lugs 'gags pa med
1b4(1): pa'i dbang // bya ba rgyun du spyod pa'i dbang // 'das pa rjes su bzung ba'i dbang // ma 'ongs gnad la 'gel ba'i dbang // da lta smin par byed pa'i dbang // ma rdzogs rdzogs
2a1(1): par byed pa'i dbang // thams cad bzlog par byed pa'i dbang // gso byed yo byad nyid kyi dbang // 'du byed ro langs gser bsgyur dbang // thal byed ro bsreg
2a2(1): 'khor lo'i dbang // sgrub byed ral gri mtshon cha'i dbang // smin byed sdom pa rnam bzhi'i dbang // thams cad dbang gi 'khor lor bstan pa'o// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus
2a3(1): gcig na/ rang rig b+han d+hA 'bar ba'i gzhal yas nas// bcom ldan 'das dbang thams cad kyi bdag nyid/ pad+ma he ru ka zhes bya ba bzhugs te/ de yang bcom ldan 'das de
2a4(1): nyid dbu gsum pa phyag drug pa/ zhabs bzhi bgrad pa/ sku la dur khrod kyi rgyan sna tshogs kyi brgyan pa/ glang chen gyi pags pa dang / klu rigs bzhis dbu dang yan lag brgyan pa/
2b1(1): zhing chen dang rin po che'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa/ bskal pa'i me ri sna tshogs sku las 'phro ba/ phyag na mtshon cha gar yang ma nges pa bsnams pa/ zhabs re re la lcags kyi rta rmig gsum gsum byung ba/
2b2(1): dbu re re la rta mgo ljang zhur re re rta skad phyogs bcur sgrogs pa/ zhal nas pad+ma ta kr-i ta yi sgra sgrogs pa// dbang thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid 'gro ba yongs la bskur ba/ sku mdog le brgan dbang gi
2b3(1): dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa/ zhabs kyi 'og tu ta kr-i ta khro bo chen po brgyad po brdzis pa/ lte ba na rta mgrin dmar po zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ thugs ka na gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje sku mdog sngon po/ zhal
2b4(1): gcig phyag gnyis pa/ g.yas rdo rje tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du gsor zhing / g.yon sdig 'dzub dang zhags pa bsdams pa/ dpung par hUM ka ra dkar po zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ g.yas na gsod pa'i sta re phyar
2b5(1): ba// g.yon na phur ba 'dril ba'o// rta mgo'i steng na rdo rje sems dpa' dkar po/ g.yas rdo rje rtse dgu thugs kar 'dzin pa/ g.yon dril bu dku la brten pa'o// de lta bu'i bcom ldan 'das de la/ 'khor
2b6(1): dpag tu med pa'i tshogs 'di lta ste/ pad+ma he ru ka la sogs rigs kyi khro bo lnga dang / yum krod+hi shwa ri ma dang / rdo rje sems dpa' dang / rnam par snang mdzad dang / rin chen 'byung ldan dang / snang ba mtha' yas
3a1(1): dang / don yod grub pa dang / sangs rgyas spyan ma dang / mA ma ki dang / gos dkar mo dang / dam tshig sgrol ma dang / nam mkha'i dbyings phyug ma dang / rdo rje'i rdo rje dang / rdo rje las dang / rdo rje
3a2(1): chos dang / rdo rje rnon po dang / rdo rje ral gri dang / rdo rje be con dang / rdo rje tho ba dang // rdo rje me tri'o// 'joms ma reg dang / 'joms ma yid dang / 'joms ma dri dang / 'joms ma ro dang / 'joms ma dus
3a3(1): dang / 'joms ma chen mo 'byung ba lnga dang / 'joms ma chen mo snang ba ma'o// lha dbang dang / mi dbang dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po dang / byol song gi dbang po dang / yi dwags kyi dbang po dang / dmyal ba'i

3b1(1): la gnas pa dang / bcu pa la gnas pa'i 'khor ro// klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang / 'jog po dang / mthas yas dang / dung skyong la sogs pa'o// phyag na rdo rje dang / rta mgrin dang / gshin rje gshed dang / 'jam
3b2(1): dpal dang / phyag rdor zhi ba dang / spyan ras gzigs dang / rigs kyi khro bo bsam gyi mi khyab pa'o// grul bum gyis rgyal po dang / mi'am ci'i rgyal po dang / lto 'phye'i rgyal po dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po dang /
3b3(1): dri za'i rgyal po dang / 'byung po thams cad kyi rgyal po dang / sha za'i rgyal po dang / yi dwags kyi rgyal po dang / sa la gnas pa dang / chu la gnas pa dang / rlung la gnas pa dang / me la gnas pa dang / nam mkha'
3b4(1): la gnas pa'i 'khor bsam gyis mi khyab pas bskor ba'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal chen po de nyid dregs pa can thams cad dbang du sdud pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// de nas
3b5(1): 'khor dpag tu med pa'i rigs rnams dang / thabs cig tu bzhugs so// zhes rdzogs pa rang byung chen po'i rgyud las/ gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// // @#// rgya gar skad du/
3b6(1): sarba sin d+hu hu ka ra ya sing nA ma/ bod skad du/ khrus thams cad kyi lung zhes bya ba/ bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// de nas 'khor de rnams kyi nang nas/ gsang ba'i bdag
4a1(1): nyid rdo rje rnam 'joms kyis 'di skad ces gsol to// kye kye bcom ldan dbang gi bdag/ khams gsum 'khor ba'i sems can la// rnam rtog dri ma bsam yas pas// sgrib pa rnam pa gnyis
4a2(1): sbyangs pa'i// thabs chen mtshon pa'i yan lag dang / sems can dri ma can dag gi/ rtogs pa sbyangs pa'i khrus chen dang // khrus kyi sgrub pa gsung du gsol// de nas pad+ma he ru kas// rnam 'joms nyid la bka'
4a3(1): stsal pa// kye ma rdo rje rnam 'joms nyon// ngas bstan legs par yid la zung // khrus kyis rnam rtog sbyong byed na// shin tu dben pa'i gnas dag tu// phyi mtshams tshul bzhin bya ba dang // spyi bshags la sogs
4a4(1): rab tu bya// de nas dkyil 'khor 'dom gang la// ba yi rnam lngas sbyang bar bya// tsan+dan la sogs dri zhim pos// chag chag rab tu btab nas ni// thig ni gzhung dang mthun pa ste// shin tu rgyas par gdab bya
4a5(1): ste// de nas tshon sna lnga yang dgye// dbus ni zlum po'i pho brang du// pad+ma mdzes pa 'dab brgyad bri// pad+ma lte ba sngon pos bkang // 'dab ma rnams ni mdzes tshon no// de yi phyi rol gru bzhi ste// sgo dang bcas pa
4a6(1): dag tu bri// gru chad ljang gu mdzes pa ste// sgo rnams rigs dang 'dra ba'o// sgo yi mtha' ma zlum po ste// rdo rje ra bar bcas pa bri// zlum po'i kha dog dmar po bya// bar khyams nag po dag tu bya// de nas dkyil
4b1(1): 'khor de nyid la// rdzas ni 'di ltar dgod par bya// pad+ma'i lte ba'i dkyil dag tu// bum pa mdzes pa gcig bzhag ste// tshon skud lnga yi gzung thag gdags// pad+ma'i 'dab ma re re la// lha bshos re re gzhag
4b2(1): par bya// dkyil 'khor phyogs mtshams brgyad nyid du// phur pa bcu la khro bo sngags// phyogs bcu nyid du rab tu bkod// phyogs skyong bcu la gtor ma bcu// yi dwags 'byung po'i gtor ma dang // rigs drug
4b3(1): rnams la gtor ma gcig/ chos skyong 'khor dang bcas pa dang / ma mo rnams la gtor ma gcig/ dbus su dpal gyi gtor ma bca'// sgo bzhir ral gri bzhi yang gzug/ gru bzhir mda' bzhir me long
4b4(1): bzhi// dar sna dag kyang gdags par bya// khrus chu'i bum pa gcig ni gru chad de// bum pa de dag rnams la yang // sman kyi yo byad sna tshogs dang // ka ra bu ram la sogs dang // gser dang man shel nor bu
4b5(1): dang // rin chen sna lnga ci snyed dang // rgya mtsho'i tshwa dang lan tshwa dang / tshwa sna ci snyed yod pa dang // spos dang tsan+dan gla rtsi dang // dri zhim pa yi spos rnams dang // mar dang sha dang ro zhim dang / 'bras dang nas dang
4b6(1): 'bru rnams dang // shing thog la sogs 'bras bu rnams// bum pa dag gi snying por gsungs// ras dkar dri med gtsang ma yis// mgul chings dag ni bya bar gsungs// de nas dkyil 'khor de nyid la// ras
5a1(1): dkar mdzes pas gdugs su bya// yungs kar sA lu ldang pa yis// bum pa'i kha rgyan bya bar gsungs// de nas bcom ldan dbang chen la// rnam 'joms nyid kyis yang zhus pa// kye kye bcom ldan
5a2(1): dbang chen sku// dkyil 'khor rdzas nyid de ltar na// sgom thabs mchod pa'i rim pa gsungs// bcom ldan pad+ma he ru kas// rdo rje khro bo de nyid la// stobs ldan nyid kyi bka' stsal pa// kye ma nyon cig rnam par

5a6(1): pa'o// g.yon pa gsum gyi phyag mtshan ni// bam dbyug thod pa sdigs mdzub ste// dbu yi steng na rta mgo gsum// rta skad sgrogs shing dbang skad 'tsher// me ri sna tshogs 'phro ba'i me// de lta bu yi dbang chen

5b6(1): rnams ni bum pa ste// g.yon pa rnams ni sdigs 'dzub bo// de nas bcom ldan bde chen des// rnam 'joms nyid la lung bstan pa// kye ma rdo rje rnam 'joms nyon// gsang sngags khrus kyi sgrib sbyang

10a2(1): dbang chen sku// tshe 'das sems can de dag ni// ngan song gsum nas drangs pa'i phyir// cho ga'i sbyor ba gsung du gsol// de nas pad+ma he ru kas// de dag rnams la bka' stsal pa/ de nas zhi ba'i 'dzab
10a3(1): dbyangs bgrangs// oM AHhUM badz+ra d+haM kra mr-i d+hA tI shwa ri/ lAM dwe Sha ra ti/ bai ra ga ra ti s+t+waM/ maM mo ha ra ti/ aM a ro li ka/ de skad brjod cing gzugs la bstim// yi ge de dag re re yi// 'od zer rab tu 'phos pa

304b2(1): ti'i don// ma bskyed rdzogs pa'i thig le rnam lnga gsal// 'gyur med ye shes dag pa'i phyogs dang bral// stong pa rang sangs nam mkha'i khu rlangs bzhin// 'gyur med rang dag chu yi lbu ba bzhin// rnam dag
304b3(1): mkha' mnyam rdo rje stong pa nyid// dus med lhug pa chu yi dkyil 'khor bzhin// stong pa'i don la cis kyang bskyod du med// gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor ye shes lnga dang ldan// dag pa'i ye shes tshom bu lnga dang
304b4(1): ldan// rdzogs chen gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa na// rdzogs chen don la thogs pa med par 'byung // tshig don ye shes gtan tshigs chen por bshad// yang dag ye shes zla 'od bzang // 'od chen ston ka'i

305a1(1): dag ye shes 'od dang bcas// mkha' mnyam rig pa'i sku dang bcas// stong pa rdo rje lam dang bcas// gsal ba 'od kyi dbyings su 'dus// de bzhin dgongs pa dag pa'o// e ma rdzogs chen
305a2(1): byang chub sems// mkha' mnyam rdo rje'i sku la spyod// stong pa yang dag lus la rdzogs// sems sogs 'dzin pa'i chos las grol// skye med yang dag ngo bo rnyed par gsungs// mi bskyod mkha' la rig pa

305a5(1): bcom ldan rnam dag sku// rdzogs chen rang skad de ltar na// bdag cag mos pa'i 'khor rnams la// mi g.yo mnyam gzhag gsung du gsol// zhes zhu ba zhus so// de nas yang bka' stsal pa// kye ma gsang
305a6(1): bdag rdo rje 'dzin// ngas bstan khyod kyis legs par nyon// mi g.yo mnyam gzhag dgongs pa ni// 'di ltar kun la shes par bya// mi g.yo ba ni sku yi rgyan// mi bskyod pa ni ye shes te// mi 'gag pa ni shes
305b1(1): rab bo// yang dag mi phyed mnyam gzhag go/ srog med 'dzin pa med pa nyid// bya dang byed pa'i tha tshig las// yod dang med pa'i mtha' las grol// nyon mongs spangs par mi 'dod cing // ye shes len par

305b3(1): dag don la bsgrub tu med// sgron ma'i yul la btsal du med// snang ba nyid la gzung du med// yang dag sku la blta dang bral// rang rig don la bsgrub tu med// snang ba'i yul la 'dzin du med// yon tan rtsal
305b4(1): la 'gag pa med// mtshan ma'i chos la zhe 'dod med// dag pa'i 'od zer tha snyad stong // yon tan sprul pa cir yang sprul// da lta'i rig pa chos kyi sku// ma 'ongs tshig las 'das pa'o// mngon sum mi gnas

306a1(1): bar mi 'dod chos dang bral// go ba'i yul na shes rig che// mthong ba'i yul na snang ba gsal// shes pa'i dus na yangs pa che// mthun pas gang gis chos dang bral// the tshom sgro 'dogs chos
